# G

[Back to index](index.md)

## ga

### Sense 1: lexicon

- **Pronunciation:** `GA`
- **Part of speech:** particle
- **Definition:** ongoing or habitual action
- **Register/status:** grammar; accepted
- **Domains:** daily-life
- **Literal:** grammatical particle: aspect
- **Example:** Lem ga naf bi mar.
- **Corpus:** active (6 attestations); tracks: literary-poetic, technical-software; examples in poetic-482, poetic-516, tech-021

### Sense 2: particle

- **Pronunciation:** `GA`
- **Part of speech:** particle:aspect
- **Definition:** ongoing or habitual action
- **Register/status:** aspect; accepted
- **Domains:** daily-life
- **Literal:** Marks continuing practice or repeated conduct.
- **Example:** Lem ga naf bi mar.
- **Corpus:** active (6 attestations); tracks: literary-poetic, technical-software; examples in poetic-482, poetic-516, tech-021

## gab

### Sense 1: lexicon

- **Pronunciation:** `GAB`
- **Part of speech:** verb
- **Definition:** to soil, ground, or make fertile earth
- **Register/status:** plain; accepted
- **Domains:** nature-ecology, travel-place, science-math
- **Root family:** `GB`; Nature; soil, ground, fertile earth; soil, ground, fertile earth, walked surface
- **Pattern:** verb
- **Literal:** G-B root, action vowel a
- **Example:** Na gab.
- **Corpus:** observed (2 attestations); tracks: literary-poetic; examples in poetic-019

- **Pronunciation:** `GARANAX-RET`
- **Part of speech:** noun
- **Definition:** right, claim, or protected standing concerning: grain, dry seed staple
- **Register/status:** civic; accepted
- **Domains:** nature-ecology, travel-place, science-math
- **Root family:** `GRNX`; Nature; grain, dry seed staple; grain, dry seed staple, stored field provision
- **Pattern:** right
- **Literal:** G-R-N-X root, right suffix -ret
- **Example:** Garanax-ret ret cel sak.
- **Corpus:** unattested (0 attestations)
